### Chemistry

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[x_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{+,\mathrm{chem}} = K_{\mathrm{P_1}} x_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{-,\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_{\mathrm{P_1}} = \mathbf{1}^T\]

  Variable legend: `x=[m_source,m_volatile,m_liquid,m_essence,m_fixed]^T`; `K_line` conserves total material.
  Reading: outlet fixation / timed transmutation / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.1`

  Reading: outlet fixation / timed transmutation / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed

  Reading: outlet fixation / timed transmutation / circulation circuit line.

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: outlet fixation / timed transmutation / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed
